  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=6.3)
    While the cooking metaphor is original, the language occasionally becomes overwrought ("elasticizing grief into a healing stew"). The emotional journey follows a somewhat predictable redemption arc. Several phrases feel formulaic ("bittersweet reckoning," "wavering resolve"). The story shows creativity in combining sci-fi elements with emotional healing but relies too heavily on explicitly stating the character's emotional realizations rather than revealing them through action.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=4.3)

The story's surreal elements, while interesting, sometimes serve as a substitute for deeper character development and logical progression.
